 After seeing the play my wife felt that she cried so much in the play that the next day when she went to the doctor, the doctor said that there is no need for the operation anymore
 tumhaari wo nerve khul gai he
 This was followed by his drama Godse @ Gandhi directed by Tom Altar on stage
 com kii baat uthi

 godse@gandhi
 Com gives answers to many questions
 Asgar Vajahat, while talking about his play, said that there were many performances of this drama
 marathi main, kannada main, gujarati main
 Its purpose was that this drama brings out the answers to the questions which were not answered in our society after independence, the questions which were not answered in that society
 jaise ek prashn he ki jis loktantr ko hamane sweekaar kiya kya yah uchit tha, yaa hamen khojna chahie tha kisi or tarah kaa loktantr, hamen kya karnaa chahie tha
 There was no answer to this question
 iske saath hi is sawaal kaa bhi jawaab nahin diya gaya ki kya ham vikaas kii jo paribhaasha maanate hai kya wo sahi he
 The second was a question that was very important, which was done through Gandhi and Godse, whether there was any dialogue or any interaction between the understanding of these two people
 donon hindu dharm ke maanane vaale hai
 Was there any talk between these two sides? is naatak main gandhi or godse ke madhyam se or jo paristhitiyon hai unke madhyam se yah koshish kii gai he ki vah samvaad sthapit ho baatcheet se koi rasta nikalnaa chahie jo in mul prashnon ke uttar de

 There is a need to establish dialogue even today, in the discussion, a question arose that in the social situation today, in this co-ordination where there are also those who believe in Gandhi and who are also believers of Godse, what is the dialogue going on between them, Can any outline of that dialogue be made, will there be any benefit from the dialogue, what do you think? jawaab dete hue asagar vajahat ne kaha mere naatak main gandhi or godse ek samvaad bolte hai, kehete hai
 Let me first tell that my play begins with the slaughter of Gandhi but Gandhi survives in it, Gandhi did not die, he survived
 unhone kaha ki main sabase pehle godse se milanaa chaahunga jisane mere upar goli chalaai thi
 After that Gandhiji has dialogues with Godse
 gandhi ji godse se kehete hai dekho tumne mere upar goli chalaai to kuch log tumse ghrinaa karne lage, kuch log tumse prem karne lage
 Nobody has found the path between love and hate and that middle path is the way of communication, the path of dialogue
 unhone ant main kaha ki aaj bhi samvaad sthapit karne kii hi jarurat he kyonki yahi nahin ho paa rahaa he

 logon ke bich samvaad banane vaale aaj nahin hancharcha main aage panini ne kaha ki ye jo samvaad sthapit karne kii baat he kya aisa to nahin he ki usase sthitiyaan or ulat hoti jaati hai kyonki hamane aksar dekha he ki kisi bhi tarah kaa sanchaar bahut jaldi logon ko nagavar guzarane lagata he
 i want to take you to the social side of tolerance
 sawaal kaa jawaab dete hue asagar ne kaha mujhe lagata he ki hamaare desh main satta kaa jo swaroop he vah bada nirankush hota he
 No matter who has the power, the power does not want to communicate, it wants to change right
 hamaare desh kii sattaaon ne kabhi samvaad nahin kiya
 Rather kept running his orders
 yah hameshaa hota rahaa
 That is why the situation of communication is difficult
 samvaad kii sthiti public domen main ban sakati he
 Can be made between people
 lekin logon ke bich samvaad banane vaale aaj nahin hai
 There was a time that our society had such powers
 lekin aaj public spes main aisi shakti nahin he
 Today, politics has got all the power
 samaaj ke andar vah shakti nahin bachi he jo samvaad ko chalaa sakati he
 Only the path of art and culture can take us forward
 jitne zyada ham sanvadensheel honge utana samvaad ke najadik jaaenge jitna asamvedansheel honge samvaad se dur hote jaaenge
 But there is no awareness in our country about literature and education
 aazaadee ke baad is vajah se shuru hui samvadahinataunse ek anya prashn poocha gaya ki sanchaar madhyamon kaa istemaal hindustan main pashchimon deshon ke jaise nahin hua, kya aapako lagata he ki shiksha, sahitya or samskruti ke liye koi jagah he
 When the medicine is not going in the mouth, how will it affect? asagar vajahat ne jawaab dete hue kaha ki iske liye hamen rashtriya andolan ko dekhnaa padegaa
 During the national movement we know that literature, arts and culture not only developed from the hands of foreign rulers, but many institutions were also formed and awareness was made
 jaagarukta tivi channel or media ke upar aadhaarit nahin rah sakati logon ko aage aana chahie
 After independence, this power was taken away from the people
 aazaadee ke baad samskruti or sahitya ke vikaas kii jimmedaari sarkaron ne le lee or samskruti mantralay bana diya
 With which the powers of communicationlessness increased
 miliye hamaare mehmaan seasgar vajahat ne kahani, naatak, upanyaas, yatra-vrittant, film tathaa chitrakala aadi vibhinn kshetron main mahatvapurn rachanaatmak yogadan kiya he
 He has been the chairman of the Hindi department at Jamia Millia Islamia in Delhi
 asagar vajahat ke lekhan main anek kahani sangrah, paanch upanyaas, aath naatak or kai anya rachanaaen shaamil hai
 His stories have been translated into English, Italian, Russian, French, Iranian, Uzbek, Hungarian, Polish etc
 languages
 inke naatakon kaa desh bhar main manchan or pradarshan hua he

 yani nawabon ke shahar rampur main maujuuda chunaav main kaaphi garmi dekhne ko mil sakati he

 ajam khan ne jaya pradaa koun he poochhate hue yahaan tak kah diya tha ki vah naachne-gane waalon ke munh nahin laga karte
 This enmity between the two leaders came to the fore in the 2009 Lok Sabha elections
 bhari sabha main manch se jaya pradaa ke aansu bhi har taraf surkhiyaan bane the
 However, before that there was a time when Azam Khan campaigned fiercely for him
 amar singh ke kehane par ajam khan ne hi 2004 main jaya pradaa ko rampur se chunaav ladvaya or unki jeet bhi sunishchit kii

 yahaan tak ki 2009 main ajam khan ne jaya pradaa kii samaajawaadee party se ummidavaari kaa bhi virodh kiya lekin unhen tikat mil gaya
 Azam Khan strongly opposed him in the election, despite this Jaya Prada won
 yahaan se donon netaaon kii dooriyaan or bad gayi

 haalanki, jald hi unki vaapasi ho gai or 4 disambar 2010 ko party ne unka nishkasana radd karte hue waapas bula liya

 ) shashakt chunaav pranali se loktantr majboot hota he
 In a democratic country, elections form a government
 sahi sarkaar chuni jaae iske liye jaruri he zyada se zyada matdaan ho
 Transparency should be taken care of when it comes to voting, it is also very important
 isi ko dekhte hue chunavi prakriya main tabdili hoti rahi he
 Where previously voting was done through ballot paper
 ab uski jagah electronic voting mashin (EVM) ne lee he
 The reason behind bringing evms was also to reduce the time spent in counting and save the expenditure in maintenance of ballot-filled ball boxes
 lekin iviem kii paardarshita par bhi sawaal uthne lage
 In view of this, the Election Commission brought the concept of Voter Variable Paper Audit Trail (VVPAT)
 jiske jariye matadaata ko yah pataa chalata he ki jis candidet ke liye iviem main usne batan dabaai he, vot use hi mila he
 VVPAT machines are also attached to evms for this
 kaise kaam karti he VVPAT?VVPAT mashin iviem ke saath conect hoti he
 a slip comes out of the VVPAT when the voter presses the name of a candidate in EVM and the button in front of the election symbol
 yah bataati he ki matadaata ne jis candidet ko vot kiya he, vot use hi mila he
 The VVPAT machine operates under the Direct Recording Electronic Voting System (DRE)
 7 second tak dikhti he parchiaapane kis candidet ko vot kiya he yah VVPAT mashin se nikalne vaali parchi main dikhataa he
 In this slip the voter will see the candidate's election symbol and name in the language chosen by him
 yah parchi 7 second tak dikhti he phir silband box main gir jaati he
 What happens to the slip from the VVPAT? The slip from the VVPAT falls into the machine after 7 seconds
 yah mashin puri tarah se pack or lock hoti he
 If someone thinks that he will get this slip, it is not so
 sirf poling adhikari hi VVPAT kii is parchi tak pahunch saktaa he
 On the day of counting these slips can be matched with electronic votes
 kaise hota he voton or parchi kaa milan?counting ke din voton kii ginati main kisi prakaar ke vivaad hone par pratyaashee kii maang par voton or parchi kaa milan kiya jaataa he
 Now the question arises that how does matching happen? Are each vote counted? So the answer is simple
 ek iviem main jitne vot pade hai ye counting ke din mashin kii Result batan dabaate hi pataa chal jaataa he ki kis candidet ko kitne vot mili hai
 This is how the slips of the VVPAT are counted
 isse sthiti saaf ho jaati he
 How many booths will match the slips? Earlier, in the assembly elections, slips were matched at only 1 booth in every assembly constituency, but in the 2019 Lok Sabha elections, 21 opposition parties filed petitions demanding to match 50 percent evms and vvpats
 Had
 jiske baad supreme court ne chunaav ayog ko nirdesh diya he ki loksabhaa seat ke antargat aane vaali sabhi vidhansabhaon ke 5 boothon par iviem or vivipat kaa milan kiya jaae
 Name of which candidate in EVM at which number? Learn how to decide where this VVPAT machine is made? The Supreme Court had directed the Central Government to make the electoral process simple and transparent and the questions arising on evms
 jiske baad bharat electronics limited (BEL) or electronic corporation of india limited (ECIL) ne yah mashin 2013 main banaai thi
 The same two Indian companies also manufacture evms
 sau saal lag gaye vivipat ke idia main?baat san 1890 kii he
 In the US, the voter did not know whether his vote went to the right candidate
 isi ko lekar 1897 main horeshio rogers ne nirikshan kiya tha
 In which he has found that through the direct voting machine system, the voter had no proof of where his vote went
 saal gujara or agle hi saal 1899 main joseph grey ne ek aisa mekensm bataaya jisamen mashin se voting ke vakt ek tikat nikle jise ballat box main daalane se pehle matadaata khud dekh sake
 Though the votes were still being cast by machine, he suggested the means of getting a ticket
 voting mashin main sudhaar hote gaya he or EVM tak pahunch gaya
 But there was still room for improvement over the slip
 america computer profeshnal ne uthaai thi aawajaiviem main honi vaali gadabadi ko rokane ke liye computer security prafational bruce snair (bruce Schneier) ne 1990 ke dashak main phir se aawaaj buland thi
 He is the one who demanded VVPAT
 1992 main amareki computer scientist rebeka maracuri ne joseph grey ke idia ko doharaaya
 In 2000, Mercury did his phd on Mercury Method
 isamen unhone mashin se nikalne vaali vivipat or matadaata ke bich kaanch kii diwaar kaa idia bhi diya jisase voter is parchi ko apane saath na le ja saken
 Where was the use of VVPAT for the first time? It was used in the 2002 election in the city of Sarkmento, California
 is vivipat vaali mashin ko evante intnational technology ne banaaya tha
 In the US, VVPAT is used in general elections in 27 states while 18 states adopt it only in local and assembly elections
 jabaki5 aise rajya hai jo vivipat ko nahin apanaate hai
 When did VVPAT come to India? VVPAT was first used in Nagaland election in 2013
 sitambar main hue rajya ke noksen vidhansabha seat ke liye vivipat lagi iviem kaa istemaal hua tha
 In the same year, in 10 out of 40 assembly seats in Mizoram, voters cast their votes from evms with VVPAT
 2014 main sirf 8, is baar puri siton par VVPAT2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav kii 543 siton main sirf 8 siton par vivipat kaa istemaal kiya gaya
 These seats were Lucknow, Gandhinagar, Bangalore South, Chennai Central, Jadavpur, Raipur, Patna Sahib and Mizoram
 saal 2017 main hue paanch rajyon ke vidhansabha chunaavon main ayog ne 52,000 vivipat kaa istemaal kiya
 Whereas evms with VVPAT were used in all the seats of Goa assembly elections
 2019 loksabhaa chunaav main har booth par iviem ke saath vivipat vaali mashin lagi rahegi
 Out of which the Election Commission will match the VVPAT on 20625 evms
 in deshon main he iviem par binelectronic voting mashiinon kaa istemaal kai deshon ne shuru kiya tha
 But due to questions about these machines regarding security and accuracy, they have returned to the ballot paper
 isamen netherland, italy ne bain laga diya he
 While evms have never been used in Germany, England and France, VVPAT is a distant thing
 itnaa hi nahin america jaise desh ke kai rajyon main bina paper trail vaali iviem par bain he

 The indo-pak judicial committee visited jails in Karachi, Lahore, Rawalpindi and Lahore last week
 samiti ne paaya ki kot lakhapat jail main 20, rawalpindi kii adiyaala jail main do or karachi kii malir jail main ek kaidi maansik rup se biimaar he
 The committee recommends that the severely and severely seriously ill, mentally deranged and mute deaf inmates be kept in proper hospitals or special institutions, regardless of which nation they belong to or what crime they committed
 is
 samiti ke samaksh kareeb 535 bhartiya kaidi prastut kiye gaye
 Of these, 483 fishermen (11 of whom are minors) and eight civilian prisoners are lodged in Malir District Jail in Karachi
 iske atirikt aath kaidi adiyaala jail main or 36 bhartiya kaidi kot lakhapat jail main band hai
 The committee, formed in January 2007 under the agreement between the two countries, consists of Justice (retd) AS Gill from the Indian side, MA Khan and Justice (retd) Abdul Qadir Chaudhary from the Pakistani side, Nasir Aslam Zahid and Mian Mohammad Ajmal
 tippaniyan The committee suggested that a mechanism should be established to consider compassionate and humanitarian grounds on the cases of women, minors, mentally deranged, aged and inmates suffering from serious illnesses or permanent physical disability
 iske atirikt karachi jail main band pakistani kaidiyon kii tarah bhartiya kaidiyon ko bhi maheene main kam se kam ek baar bharat main unke rishtedaron ko phone karne karne kii ijaajat di jaani chahie
 The committee noted that the names of many prisoners are missing from the list shared twice a year by Pakistan
 samajha jaataa he ki ye bhartiya kaidi hai
 It has suggested that Pakistan and India give each other a formal proof that there is no name left in the former list of prisoners, so that each party can consider every case and there is a flaw in the lists prepared by both sides
 Can be reduced

 The American diplomat had said that the Tibetans would choose the Dalai Lama's successor
 China strongly objected to this and said that no other country interfered in it, saying that it would be necessary for the Buddhist spiritual guru, the Dalai Lama, to choose the next successor
 Not any other country
 china kaa yah bayaan america ko karaara jawaab he jisamen kaha gaya tha ki nirvasit dalai lamas ke agle uttaradhikari kaa chayan tibet ke log karenge na ki beijing ke
 'the next Dalai Lama will be chosen by Tibetans', US diplomat Sam Brownback met the Dalai Lama in Dharamshala on Monday
 mulaakaat ke baad ek kaarykram main unhone kaha tha ki dalai lamas ke agle uttaradhikari ke chayan main tibeti logon kaa adhikaar he
 Quoting Radio Free Asia (RFA), Brownback said, "the selection of the Dalai Lama's successor is a matter involving the Tibetan Buddhist system and Tibetan leaders
" iskaa kisi or se sambandh nahin he na hi kisi sarkaar se
 "china's sharp reaction has intensified the search for the successor of the 84-year-old Dalai Lama
" 1959 main chini shashan ke khilaaf tibeti vidroh ke baad se hi dalai lamas nirvasit chal rahe hai or philhal unka deraa dharmashaala main he
 China has been asserting its monopoly over the selection of the next Dalai Lama
 brownbek ke bayaan par pratikriya dete hue chini videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa geng shuang ne media se kaha ki yah china kaa aantarik maamla he
 Shuang said, the Dalai Lama is in political exile who has been running anti-china activities abroad under the guise of religion for a long time
 geng shuang ne kaha, 'china dalai lamas ke kisi bhi videshi adhikariyon ke saath mulaakaat kaa virodh karata he
 The statement of the US official is in violation of the US promise that Tibet is considered a part of China and said that it should not support Tibetan independence
 china isse jude har bayanon par apana virodh darj karata he
 Shuang also said that the United States is urged to stop contacting anyone from the Dalai Lama group
 tibeti maamle main dakhlandaji or gaiyr-jimmedaarana bayanon se bhi baj aae
 Demanding the release of the Panchen Lama, Brownback urged the Chinese government to immediately release the Tibetan godman Panchen Lama Gedhun Choki Nyima or inform the world about him
 tibeti buddha system main dalai lamas ke baad duusare sthaan par panchen lamas kaa naam aata he
 China removed Choki Nyima and elected a six-year-old Benquen Erdini as the Panchen Lama, who currently occupies the post
 nyima kahaan hai iske bare main koi aadhikarik jaankaree nahin he lekin tibeti adhikariyon ke mutabik ve adhyayan kar rahe hai or saamaanya jindagi ji rahe hai
 The Delhi government has launched a diploma course in pre-school education with the aim of preparing trained personnel for the proposed 3,000 early childhood education centers in the national capital
 yah course agle shaikshanik satr se nau jila shiksha evam prashikshan sansthaanon (diiti) main shuru kiya jayega
 There will be 450 seats in the first year
 tippaniyan An official release said that the government had earlier announced the launch of the Early Childhood Education Development Program (ECED) in 3000 centers across Delhi
 pre-skool shiksha main diploma course kaa uddeshy isiidi kaarykram ke liye kshamta kaa nirmaan karnaa he
 Announcing the commencement of the course, Deputy Chief Minister Manish Sisodia said that the creation of human resources in parallel is important for the success of the government's plan to open 3000 ECED centers

 course shuru karne kii ghoshnaa karte huye up mukhyamantri manish sisodiya ne kaha ki sarkaar kii 3000 isiidi centaron ko kholane kii yojana kii safalataa ke liye samanaantar rup se maanav sansaadhan kaa nirmaan karnaa mahatvapurn he
